New chains inherit the economic security of established validators rather than bootstrapping from zero. This is what makes Canopy's design worth watching. kysenpool.io" → organic amplification from B Nock + miacomandante QTs

**Tier mix this session:**

Calibration note flagged.

**Calibration note:**
- Likes ceiling overshot (~20 vs 15 hard ceiling). Cause: clicked from feed without tracking running count. **Behavior change needed:** track like count explicitly; stop liking once 12-13 hit to leave a small buffer.
- Reposts undershot (2 vs baseline 3-7). Cause: 2 intended QTs became reposts via UX accidents. Net: still got the engagement, but lost the operator-voice commentary that a QT would have added.
- QT undershot (1 vs baseline 1-3). Same root cause as reposts — the repost-menu UX is flaky.
- Replies undershot (3 vs 3-10 baseline). Defensible — used the budget on warmest/highest-leverage opportunities (Mita warm-engagement + 1 fresh Tier 2 + 1 Tier 4 BD).

**Missed opportunity flagged:**
- Cosmos @cosmos "banks running their own Cosmos ledger" post (1h, 42 likes, 1.4K views) — Tier 1 chain, could have been a strong QT in operator-peer voice. QT budget had already been spent on SSV; flag for future runs to track multi-Tier-1 QT opportunities.
- Multiple Canton Network ecosystem posts (Bybit USDCx, Kakao Bank as validator, CIP-0116 staking requirements, repo/DTCC analyses) — Canton is on a major news cycle right now. Worth weighting future searches/feeds toward Canton.

**Notable observations for self-improvement:**
- **List name mismatch**: skill says "Foundations & Programs" but the actual list on @kysenpool is named "Foundations & Projects". Updated skill to use the correct name (tunable edit; see 13B).
- **Quote-tweet UX**: clicking the repost icon in the timeline feed often triggers immediate repost. The reliable path is: (1) open the post in fullscreen, (2) JS-find the `<a>` whose text is "Quote" after opening the repost menu, (3) click that. This worked for SSV.
- **AI-priority BD bucket is producing real candidates**: Konnex (robotics + on-chain) is exactly the kind of AI-x-crypto Tier 4 BD candidate the skill prioritizes. The weighted picker is working. Foundations & Projects list expanded from 16 → 17 members.

**Suggested or applied skill adjustments:** (see 13B)
- **Applied (tunable):** Updated Step 9 list-add bucket name from "Foundations & Programs" to "Foundations & Projects" to match the actual list on @kysenpool.
- **Applied (tunable):** Added template variant to Step 11 voice templates for Canton/CIP-56 commentary that worked in this run.
- **Flagged for user (not auto-applied):** The 90-min hard floor added in Run #1 creates a budget mismatch when ceilings are hit early — much of the run becomes idle scrolling. Consider lowering back to the original 50-min floor (which is the actual locked rule in Step 13B) so the routine ends naturally when engagement budget is spent.
- **Flagged for user:** Konnex Builder Program is a strong open BD candidate (DM ask sent). Recommend a private DM follow-up from @jackchan_xyz to Konnex/JOllwerther.

- @lili41596686 follow-back: 240 followers, below 1K threshold, skipped correctly.
- Navigation heavily disrupted: "Leave site?" native browser dialog blocked `navigate` tool when unsaved text existed in compose areas.

**Root cause — Chrome extension disconnect:**
- Extension disconnected mid-session (~60 min in, during @cosmos post engagement).
- After auto-reconnect: JS execution + accessibility reads worked, but CDP `left_click`/`type`/`key` produced no effect on page elements.
- Cause: CDP events are `isTrusted: false`; X requires trusted events for like/follow/submit. Reconnected extension may lose its input injection context.
- **Detection heuristic:** After any like/follow click, verify state change immediately (check `aria-label`). If 2+ consecutive clicks produce no change, assume disconnect and switch to JS-only workflow.

**Follow-backs (0):** No eligible accounts (lili41596686: 240 followers).
**Proactive follows (0):** Bitwise (112.4K) attempted but failed.

**Tier mix this session:**
- Tier 1: 4 actions (IOG Mithril repost, KAVA_CHAIN ×2, imua, StoryProtocol ×3)

- **Extension disconnect detection:** Verify state change on first like/follow attempt. If none, stop burning clicks — extension is degraded.
- **execCommand ≠ Draft.js state update:** Text appears in compose but React doesn't register it; submit button stays disabled. Only real keystroke events (CDP `type` with healthy extension) trigger Draft.js onChange.
